 uttar pradesh main 30,000 se adhik lekhpal rose news channel is ummid main kholte hai ki aaj hindu muslim dibet nahin hoga, unke hadtaal par baat hogi

 It has been 13 days for their strike and no one knows if the demands will be made or not
 isi bahaane pehle ham jaanate hai ki lekhpal kaam kya karte he or phir dikhaaenge kahaan kaam karte hai

 they have to do the job of measuring the land

 sarkari yojanaon ke liye zamin kii paimaaish kar unhen kabze se nikaalnaa bhi inkaa kaam he

 vaaki bahut kam he

 (input-ieenes) Before the end of the financial year, companies are asking for investment proof from the employed people
 vahiin logon main isko lekar kai tarah ke kanfusion hai
 Most people do not understand what they can give in investment proof
 to vahiin bahut aise bhi log hai jo standard didction ko lekar kanphyus hai
 Today we are going to remove this confusion in your report
 1
 Question - Why are companies seeking investment proof? Answer- Actually, through investment proof, companies get information about the investment you have made to save tax
 company aisa aapako tex zyada yaa kam dene ke jhanjhat se bachaane ke liye karti he
 In such a situation, you have to give a copy of the investment proof to your company by a certain date
 agar aapane aisa nahin kiya to aapaki selary cat sakati he
 2
 sawaal- investment pruf main kya-kya de sakate hai ?jawaab - investment pruf ke taur par apane life yaa health policy yaa phir tex seaving nivesh kii raseed deni padegi
 On the other hand, people living in rented houses have to submit the rent receipt of the house
 iske alaava home lone le rakhaa he to isse jude dastavej bhi company ko dene honge
 3
 sawaal- kya tution fees bhi de sakate hai ?jawaab - investment pruf ke taur par aap bacchon kii tution fees kii raseed bhi de jamaa kar sakate hai
 But it also has some conditions
 pehali shart ke mutabik sirf bharat sarkaar ke saath registerd skool, college yaa anya shiksha santhaan main daakhile ke samay yaa vitt varsh main kisi bhi samay bhari gai fees tex laabh ke liye maanya hai
 Apart from this, this exemption is limited to the school fees of only two children
 agar mata-pita donon hi job main hai, to ve alag-alag tareeke se is chhot kaa phayda uthaa sakate hai
 Many times parents have to deposit various types of fees in addition to tuition fees
 bataa den ki iskar kanoon, 1961 ke section 80C ke tahat tution fees par tex main chhot milti he
 4
 sawaal - standard didction kya hota he?jawaab- standard didction aapaki salanaa kamai kaa wo hissaa he, jis par aapako koi tex nahin dena hota he
 In order to take advantage of this exemption, the Income Tax Department does not ask you for any kind of document
 aasaan bhashaa main samajhen to aapako standard didction ke tahat milane vaali 40 hajaar rupee tak kii chhot kaa koi investment pruf dene kii jarurat nahin hogi
 5
 sawaal- kaise tay hoga standard didction ?jawaab- standard didction wo ek ekamusth rakam he jise selary se hui aapaki kul kamai main se gata diya jaataa he or uske baad texable inakam kii calculation kii jaati he
 For example, if your annual income is Rs 5 lakh, then you reduce this amount by Rs 40,000 (5 lakh-40 thousand = 4,60,000)
 yani aapaki 4 lakh 60 hajaar rupee kii saalaan inakam texable he
 How much standard deduction you will get will depend on the scope of the tax slab
 is calculation se samajhensalanaa inakam - 5 lakh rupestandard didction - 40,000 rupetacceble inakam - 4,60,000 rupee (5 lakh -40 hajaar)tex chhot - 2,50,000 rupee tak4,60,000-2,50,000 = 2 lakh 10 hajaar rupetex slab- 5 fisadi6
 Question- Who has benefited from the standard deduction? Answer - In the General Budget 2018, the standard deduction of 40 thousand rupees was implemented
 standard didction lagu hone se pehle medical alouns ke taur par 15 hajaar or transport alouns ke naate 19200 rupee milte the
 Together these two used to be 34,200 rupees
 ab ise standard didction kii 40 hajaar rupee se kam kar den to aapako sirf 5800 rupee kaa phayda miltaa he
 If you understand in easy language, if you fall in the tax slab of 5 percent, then your tax is only 290 rupees
 vahiin agar 10 fisadi tex bhar rahe hai to aapke 1160 rupee bachenge jabaki 30 fisadi kaa tex de rahe hai to 1740 rupee bachaa sakenge

 5 fisadi tak kaa cashbek de rahi he
 Apart from this, Fastag ensures nonstop movement of vehicles to avoid road congestion
 vahiin aapke samay kii bhi bachat hoti he
 Who can take the fastag? Everyone who has a four-wheel vehicle can take the fastag
 iske liye aapako sirf apane vaahan kaa registration certificate, aapaki ek passport sies photo, adress pruf, original ke saath-saath pioes (point of cell) / bikri karyaalay main vaahan ke saath apane kevaisi dastavej kii ek copy dena hoga
